< review>
I've spent a substantial amount of time at 3 different crossfit gyms and dropped in on many in order to find the perfect blend of community, skillful and knowledgable training, and fun! Crossfit Crown City is it for me! The Olympic lifting customized programming has helped me reach new personal records in the 8 months I've been at the gym. I can also seamlessly jump in on a crossfit class for some conditioning-  in fact I am encouraged to do so to keep my health and training well-rounded. On top of the great atmosphere, there are also various programs the gym introduces to support balanced nutrition, strength training and my personal favorite-community service through philanthropy. All of these are available and open to anyone but there is never any pressure to partake if you're not interested. I especially love this place because in the limited free time I have, it's  a "one stop shop" that supports my health, fitness, social needs, and acts in congruence with my values by supporting its community and genuinely encouraging the best version of its members. It's the playground I've always needed as an adult!< /review>

<review>Its simple. Crossfit Crown City has changed my life. Not in some dramatic way where I lost 100 lbs or came back from the brink of disease, but in a more subtle and approachable way. On paper im a pretty average fellow. I work fulltime, I got bills, family, other hobbies and obligations. Im not a super athlete but I have always tried to keep in shape and Ive always had dreams for my fitness. I worked out for years in cycles of committed attempts at bodybuilding programs only to lose steam, focus, and motivation. Not to mention a general lack of a healthy and realistic relationship to fitness. Ide go months on and months off. I hated the uncleanliness, monotony and judgement I felt¬† in the standard globo-gym. I felt interested in crossfit, but felt it was only for intense athletes and for the wealthy.

Finally one day I tried out Crossfit Crown City. Immediately I knew nothing would be the same. JB, the owner, was not pushy like I expected him to be. To the contrary he was nothing but pleasant, warm and inviting. He didn't try to sell me anything. He simply seemed interested in showing me what the gym was all about. After knowing him for a couple years now my respect for him as an owner has only grown exponentially. Ive never met a single person who cares more about his business and passion as JB. He always is looking for ways to improve the gym and bring more to its members whether it be new equipment, community social events, programs to spark motivation and balance, or simply words of encouragement and a sincere appreciation for his clients.

So from day 1 JB showed me what the gym was all about. To put it simply: Community and Personal development. Growing as an individual in strength, fitness, general mindset and developing a realistic relationship with fitness by checking the ego at the door, and focusing on truly learning where you stand, safe and proper form, and a real plan to achieve my goals. All while being supported by knowledgeable and approachable coaches that I can truly call my friends and an amazing family of people that are happy to see me and I them. Ive made better and deeper friendships through this gym than in most of my adult life, bc we all push through difficulty together and share a similar mindset of growth and community. Its like a tribe here. Something you dont just go to, to workout in crowded superficial solitude, but to legitimately be a part of something meaningful.

And thats what I mean about how Crossfit Crown City has changed my life. Its improved my relationship to fitness. Ive worked consistently towards goals and have made more gains here in months than in literally years elsewhere. I feel comfortable and truly part of a caring, postive, non-toxic community that pushes me to be better at life, not just my fitness. Its helped me better balance my life with nutrition, sleep, work, fitness, and social connection. I truly will never go back to a regular gym ever again and I am already sad for the day I ever have to leave Crossfit Crown City. I hope that day is nothing but years and years away.

If you have reservations like I did, whether it be intimidated by the sport, the cost, or anything else, I say dont be. I was too, but it was the best decision Ive made in years.< /review></record></dataset><record>

< text>
- Coaches: The owner, JB, and the rest of the coaches genuinely care about the members and are constantly striving to improve their experience and promote a sense of community. The quality of the programming and the coaching staff is what makes CFCC unique. The coaches are very welcoming, encouraging, and has a unique ability in understanding each member's needs, strengths, and limitations to better assist them in reaching not only their fitness goals but also their personal goals in life. Everyone has an outgoing, upbeat, and a positive personality that enables them to establish a strong, meaningful relation with the members. They are all very approachable and easy to relate with that it is easy for members to discuss both their fitness and personal concerns, fears, and aspirations in life with them without feeling judged in the process. In terms of experiences, the coaches are very knowledgeable and have an extensive background in not only coaching but also special focus areas such as gymnastics and Olympic weightlifting. In addition, the coaches also have a medical background so you can ensure that they are always considering the available research, safety, and your needs in the process on a daily basis. There is no such thing as too hard or too easy as the coaches have such a good relation with the members that they are always able to find a way to challenge them so that they are progressing. I started CrossFit at 150 lbs at 13% body fat and currently I am 180 lbs at 7% body fat. A big part of progress is due to the excellent programming at CFCC as well as the coaching staff to guide me along the way.

-  Environment: The moment you walk into the building, you will be amazed at the size of the facility and all the equipment that it contains. Even with the amount of equipment in the facility, there is still a lot of space. In case you need to visualize the size of it, there is enough room in the facility to run four classes of 10 to 15 people simultaneously (three in the main building and one in the back lot). Equipment are regularly replaced to ensure that the members always have access to high-quality resources.

-    Community: The larger the box, the more likely it is for clich√©s to form and for members not to be as close to one another. However, CFCC is a rare case as it is a large box, but it does not have any of those issues. At CFCC, both the coaches and members welcome all fitness levels as we believe each individual has unique experiences to contribute. This is mainly due to the management of the co-owner, JB, who operates this box with the value of individuality, acceptance, and community that have become the core values of CFCC.  All of the members at CFCC are very welcoming, supportive, and approachable. Everyone greets one another as they walk into the gym and says their bye as they walk out. Everyone supports, cheers, and encourages one another to improve themselves not only during a workout but also outside of the gym. The members at this facility have become one of my primary support network and my second family that I trust wholeheartedly and rely on for assistance when I need help outside of the gym. A lot of the members are at the peak of their careers ranging from nurses to orthopedic surgeons to therapists (a majority of the members are medical professionals) that are more than willing to help that makes CFCC so unique. On a daily basis, I always look forward to working out with the community and enjoy seeing the comradery of them cheering each other on during a workout. A lot of the members are at the peak of their careers ranging from nurses to orthopedic surgeons to therapists (a majority of the members are medical professionals) that are more than willing to help.

As descriptive as my review was, the best way to truly understand what a gym is like is to come and experience it for yourself. CFCC does offer a free trial for those that are on the edge of trying. I can guarantee you'll be having fun and making life-long friends along the way.</text>

<Text>I spent here 7 nights. It was okay, because it was relatively cheap, the public transportation was close and some of the attractions of Hollywood were also nearby. I could walk to the Hollywood sign or the Griffith Observatory in an hour. The Walk of Fame was just about 3 corners away. If you want to buy some food or drink, there are some shops just around the corner, but there is no service at all at the hotel. The room was always cleaned, the bed was always made and I got fresh towels and toiletries every day. The room was well equipped: TV, safe, alarm clock, iron, hair dryer, AC...etc were in the room. On the other hand, the noise level was a bit high. There is a busy road nearby which causes a lot of noise. The walls are very thin, so you hear if someone is walking on the corridor or in the room above you. My room did not have any view. There were windows but all I could see was a parking lot. There is a food smell on the corridor (which is not disturbing, but it is strange). The only way to get food or drink is the shops nearby. There is a vending machine at the reception, but it is very expensive.

Overall: If you come to Los Angeles, to do stuff around the city, this is a good place. For sleeping and bathroom it is very good and it is at a reasonable price point. I prefer these places, because I usually just want to have a place to sleep and take a decent shower in a private and clean place. If you come to LA to enjoy hotel services, enjoy the view, have a bar in your room and other fancy things, you might search for another place.<//Text><pics>None</pics><response>None< /response>< Gmap_id>

< Review>
If you want to experience authentic home style mexican food i would recomend this place to everyone. The mole and steak picado is very delicious. The people are friendly and treat you as a person not a customer. This place has grown in size but the food has not changed. Where i work we cater to everyone who has completes 5yrs of employment and when i get to 5yrs i will ask for Tio Chava to cater for me. Like i said this place is good! Its not like all these other americanize restaurants (albertos -el torito) to name a few.  You dont have to take my word for it. I would say come and taste for yourself.<//Review>

<Review>In a country where the local cuisine changes dramatically every 30 miles, the city of Nagpur, which is in the Vidarbha region of the western state of Maharashtra, needs special mention !

And who better to represent it than the best known chef from Nagpur ‚Äì Mr. Vishnu Manohar lovingly and respectfully called ‚ÄúVishnuji‚Äù.

And then we heard that Vishnuji is to open a Franchise of his famous global chain of restaurants ‚ÄúVishnuji ki Rasoi‚Äù in Sunnyvale CA and we eagerly looked forward to having a meal there.

At least yesterday we had the privilege to visit the new restaurant. It presently has a soft opening and they are serving limited items and that too in a buffet style.

And we were so pleased to see that the great chef himself was there, overseeing the cooking and serving of customers. What a humble man and so sweet to talk too! Ever ready to do anything to please his customers and admirers !

He was ably supported by his local partner, Sameer Patil, who seemed eager to pick up the ropes and run the place, once Vishnuji returns home next week.

The food variety itself was limited, but a morsel of each item brought back memories of authentic home cooked Maharashtrian meals - ones that your Indian aunt would make for you with love and care.

I particularly swooned over the ‚ÄúShev chi Sabji‚Äù very spicy, but mouthwateringly good !. The better half swore that ‚ÄúMasala Bhaath‚Äù was exactly how she recollected it to taste. And other acocmpanyments too were made very very well !

They expect to serve buffets for lunch with all items and a-la-carte from next Tuesday. Will look forward to coming here and tasting them.

Today‚Äôs meal had all vegetarian items (considering the soft opening and the auspicious religious festival of ‚ÄúNavratri‚Äù being celebrated back in India (Bay Area also celebrates it with equal enthusiasm at different temples around the greater Bay)!

But I would love to come back and try their Chicken Koliwada ( a favorite dish from the city of Mumbai)

< review>
We went here for lunch on a Saturday. We were told that the wait times were more than 40 minutes. While waiting, we roamed around and were called before the stipulated time.

This place though small is reminiscent of it's Pune branch. It has a rustic feel with all the brass ware and Maharashtrian utensils of the olden times. The chutney bowls are a highlight as well.

Now for the food, they have atleast 4 types of chutneys, chillies, and then the Mirchi thecha! They had mini samosas and khekda bhaji today and papads. There were 4 types of authentic Maharashtrian vegetables, two types of rice - masale bhat & plain, kadhi & two sweets.

Arguably, the mirchi in all these dishes was a bit lacking. But overall the food was awesome! Complementary paan was indeed good as well. All this for $12.99! I'm coming back for more!<//review>

< text>
Authentic Maharashtrian food, finally in the bay area. Most common choice is to take the thali and try little of several dishes. Do ask someone about the condiments to add to different dishes. They are  placed nearby. The chutneys are excellent. They have seats outside with heat lamps.

They serve poori, if you are early, you may have to wait for it. There are a few items also on the menu.

I hope this restaurant thrives. We do need variety of cuisines. I wonder if they should adopt the Rajwadi style to serve at the table, for refills. Initially just give minimum of each dish to taste.</text>

< date>
1575474331400<//date>
<rating>3< /rating>< review>
Came on a Saturday for lunch. It was PACKED. I'm not sure they were ready for such a crowd. The place is small, and there's not much room to move around.

Food. There are a lot of accompaniments which was different from the typical Indian buffet. There's a green herb paste which is incredible and fresh. The preserved lemon paste was amazing too.

Issues: there were maybe 8 dishes; 2 of them rice, 1 of them sweet. Nothing was labeled, not that it would have mattered for me, but there's always Google. Most things were empty, because again, it was PACKED. So after you navigate back to your seat after a few minutes, your food is cold and of course THAT'S when they bring out the fresh stuff. People were going back for 2nds with the same plates they already used GROSS. They ran out of the small silver dishes/bowls and gave small disposable plastic ones to use. VERY wasteful...

Honestly- a better model would be to bring everyone, everything. You could ask if they want white rice or yellow, offer seconds on anything they liked, and hold the sweet until the end. I realize this requires more staff, but honestly it would be so much smoother considering space and how few items there are.

All that said, it was tasty, I didn't miss meat, and I was grossly full until the following day. Everything was fairly salty as well. Not sure I'd be back, but always happy to try something new.< /review>

<text>I have been to this place recently and here's my experience.

I went for lunch and found there were people already waiting in queue. Since we accepted to sit outside, we were able to get the table immediately. The restaurant only serves Maharashtrian Vegetarian Buffet. It was a decent amount of space, but considering it is self-service buffet, it can feel chaotic in that limited space.

Coming to the food, this was the first time I was trying Maharashtrian cuisine, so I cannot claim for authenticity, but the menu (containing Masala Bhat, Patal Bhaji, Sev Bhaji, Khadi, etc) stood out from a typical North Indian or South Indian fare. The flavors were also delicious with each dish having a distinct base. It was also a (pleasingly) good amount of spice that you would expect out of an Indian cuisine.
